
#### animationscript function main #####
# data/chars/misc/flash/flash.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==0)
    {
        if(frame==12)
        {
            suicide();
        }
        return;
    }

}

#### animationscript function main #####
# data/chars/misc/dust/dust.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==13)
    {
        if(frame==7)
        {
            suicide();
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==14)
    {
        if(frame==1)
        {
            sampleRandom("crowd", 5, "crowd2", 5, 0);
        }
        if(frame==8)
        {
            suicide();
        }
        return;
    }

}

            leaper(0, 0.5, 0);
        }

}

#### animationscript function main #####
# data/chars/misc/explosion/destruction_b.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==19)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            spawn01("quakehigh", 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 0, -1, 0, -1);
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 1, 1, 0, 1);
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 0, -1, 0, 1);
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 1, 1, 0, -1);
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, -1);
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 1, -1, 0, 1);
        }
        if(frame==4)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, 1);
        }
        if(frame==4)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 1, -1, 0, -1);
        }
        if(frame==5)
        {
            suicide();
        }
        return;
    }

}

            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 1, 1, 0, 1);

        if(frame==2)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 0, -1, 0, 1);

        if(frame==2)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 1, 1, 0, -1);
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 0, 1, 0, -1);

            shoot("blast", 0, 0, 1, -1, 0, 1);

            suicide();
        }
        return;

#### animationscript function main #####
# data/chars/heroes/axel/axel.txt
########################################
void main()
{
    int frame = getlocalvar("frame");
    int animhandle = getlocalvar("animhandle");
    if(animhandle==105)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            clearL();
        }
        if(frame==8)
        {
            looper(4, 9);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==107)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            clearL();
        }
        if(frame==8)
        {
            looper(4, 9);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==111)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            vaultStuck(40, 40, 20);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==113)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            landSafe();
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==116)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            jump(1);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==122)
    {
        if(frame==1)
        {
            spawn01("smoke", 0, 50, 0);
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==129)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            invincible(1, 1);
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            dasher(2, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            copyMove();
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            pasteMove();
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            pasteMove();
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            pasteMove();
        }
        if(frame==4)
        {
            pasteMove();
        }
        if(frame==5)
        {
            dasher(0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==5)
        {
            keyAni("attack3", "ANI_FREESPECIAL2");
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==135)
    {
        if(frame==5)
        {
            vaultFix();
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==136)
    {
        if(frame==5)
        {
            vaultFix();
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==139)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            grabStart();
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            position(0, 5, 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            position(5, -5, 5, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            position(2, -30, 25, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            depost();
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            throw(12, 2, 2, 2, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==4)
        {
            clearL();
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==140)
    {
        if(frame==0)
        {
            grabStart();
        }
        if(frame==0)
        {
            position(0, 15, 0, 0, 1);
        }
        if(frame==1)
        {
            position(3, 10, 5, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==2)
        {
            position(2, -15, 55, 0, -1);
        }
        if(frame==3)
        {
            position(2, -40, 30, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==4)
        {
            position(4, -55, -1, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==4)
        {
            spawn01("quakehigh", 0, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==5)
        {
            leaper(1, 2.5, 0);
        }
        if(frame==5)
        {
            depost();
        }
        if(frame==5)
        {
            slam(18, 2, 2, 2, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==7)
        {
            landFrame();
        }
        if(frame==8)
        {
            clearL();
        }
        return;
    }
    if(animhandle==145)
    {
        if(frame==1)
        {
            dasher(1.5, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==7)
        {
            dasher(0.5, 0, 0);
        }
        if(frame==9)
